heading \"What are K_P quants?\" [level=2] [ref=f6e839]:\n            - link [ref=f6e840] [cursor=pointer]:\n              - /url: \"#what-are-k_p-quants\"\n              - img [ref=f6e842]\n            - generic [ref=f6e844]: What are K_P quants?\n          - paragraph [ref=f6e845]: K_P (\"Perfect\") quants are HauhauCS custom quantizations that use model-specific analysis to selectively preserve quality where it matters most. Each model gets its own optimized quantization profile.\n          - paragraph [ref=f6e846]: A K_P quant effectively bumps quality up by 1-2 quant levels at only ~5-15% larger file size than the base quant. Fully compatible with llama.cpp, LM Studio, and any GGUF-compatible runtime — no special builds needed.\n          - paragraph [ref=f6e847]:\n            - strong [ref=f6e848]: \"Note:\"\n            - text: K_P quants may show as \"?\" in LM Studio's quant column. This is a display issue only — the model loads and runs fine.\n          - heading \"Specs\" [level=2] [ref=f6e849]:\n            - link [ref=f6e850] [cursor=pointer]:\n              - /url: \"#specs\"\n              - ### Tool call: browser_evaluate
- Args
```json
{
  "function": "() => {\n  // Extract model information from the page\n  const modelTitle = document.querySelector('h1')?.textContent || '';\n  const paramText = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('*'))\n    .find(el => el.textContent?.includes('parameters') || el.textContent?.includes('params'))?.textContent || '';\n  const sizeText = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('*'))\n    .find(el => el.textContent?.includes('size') || el.textContent?.includes('download') || el.textContent?.includes('files'))?.textContent || '';\n  \n  // Look for GGUF files\n  const ggufLinks = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a'))\n    .filter(a => a.href?.includes('.gguf') || a.textContent?.includes('GGUF'))\n    .map(a => a.href);\n  \n  return {\n    modelTitle,\n    paramText,\n    sizeText,\n    ggufLinks: ggufLinks.slice(0, 10) // Limit to first 10\n  };\n}"
}
```

Specs Recommended Settings Usage Other Models    \\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive\\n\\t\\n\\n\\nJoin the Discord for updates, roadmaps, projects, or just to chat.\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B uncensored by HauhauCS. 0/465 Refusals.\\n\\nHuggingFace's \\\"Hardware Compatibility\\\" widget doesn't recognize K_P quants — it may show fewer files than actually exist. Click \\\"View +X variants\\\" or go to Files and versions to see all available downloads.\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tAbout\\n\\t\\n\\nNo changes to datasets or capabilities. Fully functional, 100% of what the original authors intended - just without the refusals.\\nThese are meant to be the best lossless uncensored models out there.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tAggressive Variant\\n\\t\\n\\nStronger uncensoring — model is fully unlocked and won't refuse prompts. May occasionally append short disclaimers (baked into base model training, not refusals) but full content is always generated.\\nFor a more conservative uncensor that keeps some safety guardrails, check the Balanced variant when it's available.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tDownloads\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\nFile\\nQuant\\nBPW\\nSize\\n\\n\\n\\t\\t\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q8_K_P.gguf\\nQ8_K_P\\n10.06\\n44 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ8_0\\n8.5\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q6_K_P.gguf\\nQ6_K_P\\n7.07\\n31 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ6_K\\n6.6\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q5_K_P.gguf\\nQ5_K_P\\n6.47\\n28 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ5_K_M\\n5.7\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_P.gguf\\nQ4_K_P\\n5.40\\n23 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_M.gguf\\nQ4_K_M\\n4.88\\n21 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ4_NL.gguf\\nIQ4_NL\\n4.56\\n20 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ4_XS.gguf\\nIQ4_XS\\n4.32\\n19 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q3_K_P.gguf\\nQ3_K_P\\n4.39\\n19 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ3_K_M\\n3.9\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ3_M.gguf\\nIQ3_M\\n3.56\\n15 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q2_K_P.gguf\\nQ2_K_P\\n3.46\\n15 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ2_M.gguf\\nIQ2_M\\n2.69\\n11 GB\\n\\n\\nmmproj-Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-f16.gguf\\nmmproj (f16)\\n—\\n899 MB\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\nAll quants generated with importance matrix (imatrix) for optimal quality preservation on abliterated weights.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tWhat are K_P quants?\\n\\t\\n\\nK_P (\\\"Perfect\\\") quants are HauhauCS custom quantizations that use model-specific analysis to selectively preserve quality where it matters most. Each model gets its own optimized quantization profile.\\nA K_P quant effectively bumps quality up by 1-2 quant levels at only ~5-15% larger file size than the base quant. Fully compatible with llama.cpp, LM Studio, and any GGUF-compatible runtime — no special builds needed.\\nNote: K_P quants may show as \\\"?\\\" in LM Studio's quant column. This is a display issue only — the model loads and runs fine.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tSpecs\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n35B total parameters, ~3B active per forward pass (MoE)\\n256 experts, 8 routed per token\\nHybrid architecture: linear attention + full softmax attention (3:1 ratio)\\n40 layers\\n262K native context\\nNatively multimodal (text, image, video)\\nBased on Qwen/Qwen3.6-35B-A3B\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tRecommended Settings\\n\\t\\n\\nFrom the official Qwen authors:\\nThinking mode (default):\\n\\nGeneral: temperature=1.0, top_p=0.95, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=1.5\\nCoding/precise tasks: temperature=0.6, top_p=0.95, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=0\\n\\nNon-thinking mode:\\n\\nGeneral: temperature=0.7, top_p=0.8, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=1.5\\nReasoning tasks: temperature=1.0, top_p=1.0, top_k=40, min_p=0, presence_penalty=2.0\\n\\nImportant:\\n\\nKeep at least 128K context to preserve thinking capabilities\\nUse --jinja flag with llama.cpp for proper chat template handling\\nVision support requires the mmproj file alongside the main GGUF\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tUsage\\n\\t\\n\\nWorks with llama.cpp, LM Studio, Jan, koboldcpp, and other GGUF-compatible runtimes.\\nllama-cli -m Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_P.gguf \\\\\\n  --mmproj mmproj-Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-f16.gguf \\\\\\n  --jinja -c 131072 -ngl Specs Recommended Settings Usage Other Models    \\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive\\n\\t\\n\\n\\nJoin the Discord for updates, roadmaps, projects, or just to chat.\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B uncensored by HauhauCS. 0/465 Refusals.\\n\\nHuggingFace's \\\"Hardware Compatibility\\\" widget doesn't recognize K_P quants — it may show fewer files than actually exist. Click \\\"View +X variants\\\" or go to Files and versions to see all available downloads.\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tAbout\\n\\t\\n\\nNo changes to datasets or capabilities. Fully functional, 100% of what the original authors intended - just without the refusals.\\nThese are meant to be the best lossless uncensored models out there.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tAggressive Variant\\n\\t\\n\\nStronger uncensoring — model is fully unlocked and won't refuse prompts. May occasionally append short disclaimers (baked into base model training, not refusals) but full content is always generated.\\nFor a more conservative uncensor that keeps some safety guardrails, check the Balanced variant when it's available.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tDownloads\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\nFile\\nQuant\\nBPW\\nSize\\n\\n\\n\\t\\t\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q8_K_P.gguf\\nQ8_K_P\\n10.06\\n44 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ8_0\\n8.5\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q6_K_P.gguf\\nQ6_K_P\\n7.07\\n31 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ6_K\\n6.6\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q5_K_P.gguf\\nQ5_K_P\\n6.47\\n28 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ5_K_M\\n5.7\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_P.gguf\\nQ4_K_P\\n5.40\\n23 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_M.gguf\\nQ4_K_M\\n4.88\\n21 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ4_NL.gguf\\nIQ4_NL\\n4.56\\n20 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ4_XS.gguf\\nIQ4_XS\\n4.32\\n19 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q3_K_P.gguf\\nQ3_K_P\\n4.39\\n19 GB\\n\\n\\n—\\nQ3_K_M\\n3.9\\n—\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ3_M.gguf\\nIQ3_M\\n3.56\\n15 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q2_K_P.gguf\\nQ2_K_P\\n3.46\\n15 GB\\n\\n\\nQwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-IQ2_M.gguf\\nIQ2_M\\n2.69\\n11 GB\\n\\n\\nmmproj-Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-f16.gguf\\nmmproj (f16)\\n—\\n899 MB\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\nAll quants generated with importance matrix (imatrix) for optimal quality preservation on abliterated weights.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tWhat are K_P quants?\\n\\t\\n\\nK_P (\\\"Perfect\\\") quants are HauhauCS custom quantizations that use model-specific analysis to selectively preserve quality where it matters most. Each model gets its own optimized quantization profile.\\nA K_P quant effectively bumps quality up by 1-2 quant levels at only ~5-15% larger file size than the base quant. Fully compatible with llama.cpp, LM Studio, and any GGUF-compatible runtime — no special builds needed.\\nNote: K_P quants may show as \\\"?\\\" in LM Studio's quant column. This is a display issue only — the model loads and runs fine.\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tSpecs\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n35B total parameters, ~3B active per forward pass (MoE)\\n256 experts, 8 routed per token\\nHybrid architecture: linear attention + full softmax attention (3:1 ratio)\\n40 layers\\n262K native context\\nNatively multimodal (text, image, video)\\nBased on Qwen/Qwen3.6-35B-A3B\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tRecommended Settings\\n\\t\\n\\nFrom the official Qwen authors:\\nThinking mode (default):\\n\\nGeneral: temperature=1.0, top_p=0.95, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=1.5\\nCoding/precise tasks: temperature=0.6, top_p=0.95, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=0\\n\\nNon-thinking mode:\\n\\nGeneral: temperature=0.7, top_p=0.8, top_k=20, min_p=0, presence_penalty=1.5\\nReasoning tasks: temperature=1.0, top_p=1.0, top_k=40, min_p=0, presence_penalty=2.0\\n\\nImportant:\\n\\nKeep at least 128K context to preserve thinking capabilities\\nUse --jinja flag with llama.cpp for proper chat template handling\\nVision support requires the mmproj file alongside the main GGUF\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tUsage\\n\\t\\n\\nWorks with llama.cpp, LM Studio, Jan, koboldcpp, and other GGUF-compatible runtimes.\\nllama-cli -m Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-Q4_K_P.gguf \\\\\\n  --mmproj mmproj-Qwen3.6-35B-A3B-Uncensored-HauhauCS-Aggressive-f16.gguf \\\\\\n  --jinja -c 131072 -ngl ### Tool call: browser_evaluate
- Args
```json
{
  "function": "() => {\n  // Extract model information from the page\n  const modelTitle = document.querySelector('h1')?.textContent?.trim() || '';\n  const tags = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('span.tag'))\n    .map(span => span.textContent.trim())\n    .filter(tag => tag.length > 0);\n  \n  // Look for size information\n  const sizeText = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('*'))\n    .find(el => el.textContent?.includes('Size') || el.textContent?.includes('Download'))?.textContent || '';\n  \n  // Look for GGUF quantizations\n  const ggufLinks = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('a'))\n    .filter(a => a.href?.includes('.gguf'))\n    .slice(0, 5)\n    .map(a => {\n      const text = a.textContent?.trim() || '';\n      const sizeMatch = text.match(/(\\d+(?:\\.\\d+)?\\s*(?:GB|MB))/);\n      return { text: text.split('\\n')[0]?.trim(), size: sizeMatch ? sizeMatch[1] : null };\n    });\n  \n  return {\n    modelTitle,\n    tags,\n    sizeText,\n    ggufLinks\n  };\n}"
}
```

The result reasons in the open (edge cases, complexity, approach) and then\\nemits a clean, runnable solution. 💚\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t📌 Announcements\\n\\t\\n\\n🚀🔥 IT'S HERE — v2 is OUT NOW! v2 has shipped — the GGUF quants are live and ready to run →\\ngrab v2 here. 🎉\\nThe full safetensors master (build / fine-tune on top) goes up tomorrow. v2 is agentic + coding focused —\\nthe piece v1 was missing.\\nHere's the result that got me most excited. When I saw v2's tau2-bench telecom result — an agentic tool-use\\nbenchmark where the model has to diagnose → fix → verify, exactly like real terminal/debugging work — I literally got\\nlaunched out of my chair (…okay, kidding 😄). The jump in actually solving the problem is wild:\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\ntau2-bench telecom · local, same harness, Q8_0\\nscore\\n\\n\\n\\t\\t\\nofficial gemma-4-12B-it (base)\\n~15%\\n\\n\\n🟢 v2 (this release)\\n~55%\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\nThe base model tends to give up early (hands the problem off to a human); v2 keeps going and works it the way a\\nmuch bigger model would. Full benchmark details are in the v2 card now. 🔧\\n✅ safetensors master (this v1 model) is UP. Full-precision weights are live →\\nyuxinlu1/gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-composer2.5-v1\\n— roll your own GGUF / MLX / AWQ quants or fine-tune straight from the master. 🎉\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t📣 Context length fixed: now 256K (was 131K) — thanks, community! 💚\\n\\t\\n\\nA community member spotted that this model was reporting only a 131K context window. That turned out to be\\nthe well-known upstream Gemma 4 metadata bug — Google's initial config.json shipped with\\nmax_position_embeddings: 131072 instead of the real 262144 (256K), and that value got baked into a lot of\\ndownstream finetunes and quants (including this one) before it was fixed upstream.\\nThe weights were always fine — it was purely a metadata field. All GGUF quants have been re-patched to the\\nfull 256K context (gemma4.context_length = 262144). Just re-download if you grabbed an earlier copy. 🙏\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t📚 Training data (the interesting part 🍳)\\n\\t\\n\\nThis is a distillation of two complementary chain-of-thought sources, both over verifiable Python coding tasks\\n(algorithmic / function-level problems that come with deterministic tests):\\n\\n🥇 Main set — Composer 2.5 real CoT. Genuine, model-authored reasoning traces. The teacher solved each problem,\\nits code was run against the task's tests, and only the passing solutions were kept. So the reasoning you're\\nlearning from leads to code that actually works.\\n🥈 Aux set — Fable 5 (released today! 🎉). A clever twist: we took the problems where Composer 2.5 got it wrong\\nand handed them to Fable 5 to redo — re-deriving a fresh, self-consistent chain-of-thought and a correct\\nsolution, again gated on passing the tests. This recovers the hard cases the main teacher missed. These traces\\nare synthetic (rationalized CoT), and are tagged separately so the two sources stay distinguishable.\\n\\nThe recipe: real CoT for the bulk of solid coverage, plus synthetic \\\"second-attempt\\\" CoT to patch the failures —\\nboth verified by execution before anything entered training. ✅\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t📦 Pick your size (GGUF quants)\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\nQuant\\nSize\\nVibe\\n\\n\\n\\t\\t\\n🟢 Q2_K\\n4.5 GB\\ntiniest — runs almost anywhere\\n\\n\\n🟡 Q3_K_M\\n5.7 GB\\ngreat for 8 GB VRAM — much better than Q2\\n\\n\\n🔵 Q4_K_M\\n6.87 GB\\nthe sweet spot 👌 (recommended)\\n\\n\\n🟣 Q6_K\\n9.11 GB\\nnear-lossless\\n\\n\\n⚪ Q8_0\\n11.8 GB\\nbasically full quality\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t🧮 \\\"Will it fit?\\\" — context length cheat-sheet\\n\\t\\n\\nRough estimates 🤓 (assumes q8_0 KV cache + ~1.5 GB overhead; use q4_0 KV cache for ≈2× more context!).\\nMax context is 256K. \\\"—\\\" = won't fit, pick a smaller quant. ✂️\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\nYour VRAM / unified mem\\n🟢 Q2_K (4.5G)\\n🟡 Q3_K_M (5.7G)\\n🔵 Q4_K_M (6.87G)\\n🟣 Q6_K (9.11G)\\n⚪ Q8_0 (11.8G)\\n\\n\\n\\t\\t\\n8 GB\\n~16K ctx\\n~10K\\ntight (~2–4K)\\n—\\n—\\n\\n\\n12 GB\\n~48K\\n~38K\\n~30K\\n~12K\\n—\\n\\n\\n16 GB\\n~80K\\n~72K\\n~64K\\n~44K\\n~22K\\n\\n\\n24 GB\\n~200K\\n~160K\\n~128K\\n~110K\\n~88K\\n\\n\\n32 GB\\n256K (max) 🎉\\n256K\\n256K\\n~230K\\n~190K\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n💡 Apple Silicon / integrated GPUs with unified memory count too — same numbers, just slower than a dGPU.\\n💡 Low on room? Drop a quant or switch KV cache to q4_0 and your context roughly doubles.\\n\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t🚀 How to run it (super easy)\\n\\t\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tOption A — llama.cpp (recommended) 🦙\\n\\t\\n\\n\\nGrab a quant above (e.g. …-Q4_K_M.gguf) and llama-server from llama.cpp.\\n⚠️ Needs a recent llama.cpp (this is the gemma4_unified architecture — older builds won't load it).\\n\\n\\nRun a server (Windows .bat shown — tweak --port, --ctx-size to taste):\\n\\n@echo off\\ncd /d C:\\\\llama.cpp\\nllama-server.exe ^\\n  -m C:\\\\models\\\\gemma4-coding-Q4_K_M.gguf ^\\n  --ctx-size 16384 ^\\n  --n-gpu-layers 99 ^\\n  --no-mmap ^\\n  -fa on ^\\n  --cache-type-k q8_0 --cache-type-v q8_0 ^\\n  --temp 1.0 --top-p 0.95 --top-k 64 ^\\n  --host 0.0.0.0 --port 18080\\npause\\n\\n\\nOpen http://localhost:18080 and chat. 🎉  (Tip: bump --ctx-size per the table; use q4_0 KV for more.)\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\tOption B — one-click apps 🖱️\\n\\t\\n\\nWorks in LM Studio, Jan, Ollama, etc. — just import the GGUF, pick your quant, go. 🐾\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t🧠 Thinking mode\\n\\t\\n\\nThis model thinks in Gemma's native thought channel before answering — exactly how it was trained. Keep\\nenable_thinking=true (the default chat template handles it). Recommended sampling: temp 1.0, top_p 0.95, top_k 64.\\nFor coding you can also go greedy (temp 0) for more deterministic solutions.\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t⚠️ Good to know\\n\\t\\n\\n\\nReduced refusals: the training data is task-focused with no safety hedging, so this refuses less than the base\\nmodel. It is not safety-aligned — add your own guardrails for production. Use responsibly. 🙏\\nSpecialized for Python / algorithmic coding. Reasoning quality is strongest in that domain; general-knowledge\\nfacts/numbers should still be double-checked.\\nEnglish-centric.\\n\\n\\n\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\n\\t\\t📚 Base & License\\n\\t\\n\\n\\nLicense: Apache 2.0. Gemma 4 is released by Google under\\nApache 2.0 (unlike the older Gemma 1/2/3 terms), so this fine-tune is\\nApache 2.0 too — free to use, modify, and redistribute. 🎉\\nBase model: google/gemma-4-12B-it.\\nPersonal/hobby project — shared as-is, no warranty. Have fun, and happy hacking! 🐾✨\\n\\n  Downloads last month 674,977  \\n\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t     GGUF Model size 12B params Architecture gemma4  Chat template  Hardware compatibility Log In to add your hardware 2-bit  Q2_K  4.83 GB 3-bit  Q3_K_M  6.09 GB 4-bit  Q4_K_M  7.38 GB 6-bit  Q6_K  9.79 GB 8-bit  Q8_0  12.7 GB         Inference Providers NEW    Text Generation     This model isn't deployed by any Inference Provider. 🙋 1 Ask for provider support     Model tree for yuxinlu1/gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-composer2.5-v1-GGUF  Base model  google/gemma-4-12B  Finetuned   google/gemma-4-12B-it  Quantized (220)  this model   Finetunes   5 models  Quantizations   5 models    Spaces using yuxinlu1/gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-composer2.5-v1-GGUF 13 💬 cl4ude/fable5  💬 karmaoriginal/fable5  🤗 shanghsin/gemma-4-12B  💬 mixtao/fable5  💬 fdrm/gemma4-fable5  🤗 shanghsin/gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-yuxinlu1  🤗 usermma/gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-yuxinlu1  🤗 jussix/Gemma-4-12B-coder-fable5-Q4-2   + 8 Spaces + 5 Spaces       System theme     Company TOS Privacy About Careers  Website Models Datasets Spaces Pricing Docs\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\t import(\\\"\\\\/front\\\\/build\\\\/kube-9565739\\\\/index.js\\\"); window.moonSha = \\\"kube-9565739\\\\/\\\"; window.__hf_deferred =\\n\\t\\t\\t{};\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\t\\tif ([\\\"hf.co\\\", \\\"huggingface.co\\\"].includes(window.location.hostname)) {\\n\\t\\t\\t\\tconst script = document.createElement(\\\"script\\\");\\n\\t\\t\\t\\tscript.src = \\\"https://js.stripe.com/v3/\\\";\\n\\t\\t\\t\\tscript.async = true;\\n\\t\\t\\t\\tdocument.head.appendChild(script);\\n\\t\\t\\t}\\n\\t\\t\\n\\t\\n\\nInference providers allow you to run inference using different serverless providers.\",\n  \"ggufLinks\": []\n}",
  "code": "await page.evaluate('() => {\\n  // Extract model information from the page\\n  const modelTitle = document.querySelector(\\'h1\\')?.textContent?.trim() || \\'\\';\\n  const tags = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(\\'span.tag\\'))\\n    .map(span => span.textContent.trim())\\n    .filter(tag => tag.length > 0);\\n  \\n  // Look for size information\\n  const sizeText = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(\\'*\\'))\\n    .find(el => el.textContent?.includes(\\'Size\\') || el.textContent?.includes(\\'Download\\'))?.textContent || \\'\\';\\n  \\n  // Look for GGUF quantizations\\n  const ggufLinks = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll(\\'a\\'))\\n    .filter(a => a.href?.includes(\\'.gguf\\'))\\n    .slice(0, 5)\\n    .map(a => {\\n      const text = a.textContent?.trim() || \\'\\';\\n      const sizeMatch = text.match(/(\\\\d+(?:\\\\.\\\\d+)?\\\\s*(?:GB|MB))/);\\n      return { text: text.split(\\'\\\\n\\')[0]?.trim(), size: sizeMatch ? sizeMatch[1] : null };\\n    });\\n  \\n  return {\\n    modelTitle,\\n    tags,\\n    sizeText,\\n    ggufLinks\\n  };\\n}');"
}
```
